HOME


The Paramony
An internet version of Biblical References for The Urantia Book
by Duane Faw

Key to Column Headings

1  Pg.Ppg — Refers to page numbering in Urantia Foundation editions of The Urantia Book. Paragraphs are numbered with the first full paragraph from the top of the page and are numbered sequentially down the page.
2  P:S.p — Refers to Paper number, section number within the paper, and the paragraph number within the section. The P:S.p links to the referenced paragraph of the Standardized version of The Urantia Book.
3  Key Words — The words or concepts which, in the mind of the author, connect the Bible and The Urantia Book.
4  Bible Notation — Bible book, such as 1 Corinthians, chapter, and verse numbers. The Bible notation links to the referenced book, chapter and verse of the King James translation of the Bible.
5  Class — Categorizations for references in which:
S = "Same" — Both books recite the same incident.
R = "Refer" — One book quotes from, or refers to an incident contained in, the other.
C = "Compare" — One book relates matter which, although not the same as the other, is significant to reinforce, modify or contradict the other.
